    1                                                //-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    2                                                // Project      : APB VIP - Advanced Peripheral Bus Verification IP
    3                                                // File         : apb_coverage.svh
    4                                                // Description  : Coverage collector for APB protocol verification
    5                                                // Author       : CH Bhanu Prakash
    6                                                // Notes        : Functional coverage collection with comprehensive analysis
    7                                                //-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    8                                                
    9                                                `ifndef _APB_COVERAGE_
    10                                               `define _APB_COVERAGE_
    11                                               
    12                                               `include "uvm_macros.svh"
    13                                               import uvm_pkg::*;
    14                                               import apb_common_pkg::*;
    15                                               
    16                                               class apb_coverage extends uvm_component;
    17              1                          4         `uvm_component_utils(apb_coverage)
    17              2                        208     
    17              3                          4     
    18                                               
    19                                                   // Analysis import to receive transactions
    20                                                   uvm_analysis_imp #(apb_base_seq_item, apb_coverage) analysis_imp;
    21                                               
    22                                                   // Coverage sampling fields
    23                                                   bit         tr_type;           // Transaction type (0=READ, 1=WRITE)
    24                                                   bit [31:0]  addr;              // Transaction address
    25                                                   bit [31:0]  data;              // Transaction data
    26                                                   bit         psel;              // Select signal state
    27                                                   bit         penable;           // Enable signal state
    28                                                   bit         pwrite;             // Write direction state
    29                                                   bit         pready;             // Ready signal state
    30                                                   bit         reset_n;           // Reset signal state
    31                                                   int         delay;              // Inter-transaction delay
    32                                                   int         protocol_phase;      // Current protocol phase
    33                                                   int         reset_transition;    // Reset transition type
    34                                                   int         back_to_back_transfers; // Consecutive transfer counter
    35                                                   int         transfer_duration;   // Transfer duration measurement
    36                                               
    37                                                   // Main transaction coverage group
    38                                                   covergroup apb_transaction_cg;
    39                                                       TR_TYPE: coverpoint tr_type {
    40                                                           bins WRITE = {1};        // Write transactions
    41                                                           bins READ  = {0};        // Read transactions
    42                                                       }
    43                                                       ADDRESS: coverpoint addr {
    44                                                           bins LOW_ADDRESSES  = {[32'h00000000 : 32'h0000FFFF]};  // Low address range
    45                                                           bins MID_ADDRESSES  = {[32'h00010000 : 32'h7FFFFFFF]};  // Mid address range
    46                                                           bins HIGH_ADDRESSES = {[32'h80000000 : 32'hFFFFFFFF]};  // High address range
    47                                                           bins WORD_ALIGNED   = {[32'h00000000 : 32'hFFFFFFFF]} iff (addr[1:0] == 2'b00); // Word-aligned addresses
    48                                                       }
    49                                                       DATA: coverpoint data {
    50                                                           bins ZERO_DATA      = {32'h00000000};  // All zeros
    51                                                           bins ONES_DATA      = {32'hFFFFFFFF};  // All ones
    52                                                           bins ALTERNATE_1010 = {32'hAAAAAAAA};  // Alternating pattern
    53                                                           bins RANDOM_DATA    = {[32'h00000001 : 32'hFFFFFFFE]};  // Random range
    54                                                       }
    55                                                       TR_TYPE_X_ADDR: cross TR_TYPE, ADDRESS {
    56                                                           bins WRITE_LOW  = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(ADDRESS.LOW_ADDRESSES);  // Write to low addresses
    57                                                           bins WRITE_MID  = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(ADDRESS.MID_ADDRESSES);  // Write to mid addresses
    58                                                           bins WRITE_HIGH = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(ADDRESS.HIGH_ADDRESSES); // Write to high addresses
    59                                                           bins READ_LOW   = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(ADDRESS.LOW_ADDRESSES);   // Read from low addresses
    60                                                           bins READ_MID   = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(ADDRESS.MID_ADDRESSES);   // Read from mid addresses
    61                                                           bins READ_HIGH  = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(ADDRESS.HIGH_ADDRESSES);  // Read from high addresses
    62                                                       }
    63                                                       TR_TYPE_X_DATA: cross TR_TYPE, DATA {
    64                                                           bins WRITE_ZERO  = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(DATA.ZERO_DATA);  // Write zeros
    65                                                           bins WRITE_ONES  = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(DATA.ONES_DATA);  // Write ones
    66                                                           bins WRITE_ALT   = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(DATA.ALTERNATE_1010); // Write alternating
    67                                                           bins WRITE_RAND  = binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE) && binsof(DATA.RANDOM_DATA); // Write random
    68                                                           bins READ_ZERO   = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(DATA.ZERO_DATA);   // Read zeros
    69                                                           bins READ_ONES   = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(DATA.ONES_DATA);   // Read ones
    70                                                           bins READ_ALT    = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(DATA.ALTERNATE_1010); // Read alternating
    71                                                           bins READ_RAND   = binsof(TR_TYPE.READ)  && binsof(DATA.RANDOM_DATA); // Read random
    72                                                       }
    73                                                   endgroup
    74                                               
    75                                                   // Protocol state coverage group
    76                                                   covergroup apb_protocol_cg;
    77                                                       TR_TYPE: coverpoint tr_type {
    78                                                           bins WRITE = {1};  // Write transactions
    79                                                           bins READ  = {0};  // Read transactions
    80                                                       }
    81                                                       PSEL_STATE: coverpoint psel {
    82                                                           bins LOW  = {0};  // Peripheral not selected
    83                                                           bins HIGH = {1};  // Peripheral selected
    84                                                       }
    85                                                       PENABLE_STATE: coverpoint penable {
    86                                                           bins LOW  = {0};  // Protocol not enabled
    87                                                           bins HIGH = {1};  // Protocol enabled
    88                                                       }
    89                                                       PWRITE_STATE: coverpoint pwrite {
    90                                                           bins LOW  = {0};  // Read operation
    91                                                           bins HIGH = {1};  // Write operation
    92                                                       }
    93                                                       PROTOCOL_PHASES: coverpoint protocol_phase {
    94                                                           bins IDLE   = {0};  // IDLE phase
    95                                                           bins SETUP  = {1};  // SETUP phase
    96                                                           bins ACCESS = {2};  // ACCESS phase
    97                                                       }
    98                                                       STATE_TRANSITIONS: coverpoint {psel, penable} {
    99                                                           bins IDLE_TO_SETUP   = (2'b00 => 2'b10);  // IDLE to SETUP transition
    100                                                          bins SETUP_TO_ACCESS = (2'b10 => 2'b11); // SETUP to ACCESS transition
    101                                                          bins ACCESS_TO_IDLE  = (2'b11 => 2'b00); // ACCESS to IDLE transition
    102                                                      }
    103                                                      PHASE_X_TR_TYPE: cross PROTOCOL_PHASES, TR_TYPE {
    104                                                          bins IDLE_WRITE   = binsof(PROTOCOL_PHASES.IDLE)   && binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE); // IDLE phase write
    105                                                          bins IDLE_READ    = binsof(PROTOCOL_PHASES.IDLE)   && binsof(TR_TYPE.READ);  // IDLE phase read
    106                                                          bins SETUP_WRITE  = binsof(PROTOCOL_PHASES.SETUP) && binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE); // SETUP phase write
    107                                                          bins SETUP_READ   = binsof(PROTOCOL_PHASES.SETUP) && binsof(TR_TYPE.READ);  // SETUP phase read
    108                                                          bins ACCESS_WRITE = binsof(PROTOCOL_PHASES.ACCESS) && binsof(TR_TYPE.WRITE); // ACCESS phase write
    109                                                          bins ACCESS_READ  = binsof(PROTOCOL_PHASES.ACCESS) && binsof(TR_TYPE.READ); // ACCESS phase read
    110                                                      }
    111                                                  endgroup
    112                                              
    113                                                  // Reset behavior coverage group
    114                                                  covergroup apb_reset_cg;
    115                                                      RESET_STATE: coverpoint reset_n {
    116                                                          bins ACTIVE   = {0};  // Reset not asserted
    117                                                          bins INACTIVE = {1};  // Reset asserted
    118                                                      }
    119                                                      RESET_TRANSITIONS: coverpoint reset_transition {
    120                                                          bins RESET_ASSERT   = (1 => 0);  // Reset assertion transition
    121                                                          bins RESET_DEASSERT = (0 => 1);  // Reset deassertion transition
    122                                                      }
    123                                                      ACTIVITY_DURING_RESET: coverpoint {reset_n, psel} {
    124                                                          bins IDLE_DURING_RESET   = {2'b00};
    125                                                          bins ACTIVE_DURING_RESET = {2'b01};
    126                                                          bins IDLE_AFTER_RESET    = {2'b10};
    127                                                          bins ACTIVE_AFTER_RESET  = {2'b11};
    128                                                      }
    129                                                  endgroup
    130                                              
    131                                                  // Timing coverage group for delay scenarios
    132                                                  covergroup apb_timing_cg;
    133                                                      TRANSFER_DELAY: coverpoint delay {
    134                                                          bins MIN_DELAY  = {1};           // Minimum delay
    135                                                          bins MAX_DELAY  = {2};           // Maximum delay
    136                                                          bins LONG_DELAY = {[3:10]};       // Long delays
    137                                                      }
    138                                                      BACK_TO_BACK: coverpoint back_to_back_transfers {
    139                                                          bins SINGLE      = {0};           // Single transfers
    140                                                          bins CONSECUTIVE = {1};         // Back-to-back transfers
    141                                                      }
    142                                                      DELAY_X_B2B: cross TRANSFER_DELAY, BACK_TO_BACK;
    143                                                  endgroup

    14                                               
    15                                                   // APB protocol signals (32-bit address and data bus)
    16                                                   logic [`ADDR_WIDTH-1:0] PADDR;     // Address bus
    17                                                   logic [`DATA_WIDTH-1:0] PWDATA;    // Write data bus
    18                                                   logic [`DATA_WIDTH-1:0] PRDATA;    // Read data bus

    26                                                       output PADDR, PSEL, PENABLE, PWRITE, PWDATA;

    28                                                   endclocking: master_cb
    29

    31              1                         52         clocking slave_cb @(posedge PCLK);
    32              1                         52             input  PADDR, PSEL, PENABLE, PWRITE, PWDATA;
    33                                                       output PRDATA, PREADY;

    39

    129                                                      apb_base_seq_item t_write, t_read, t_mis;
    130             1                          4             $display("--- force_scoreboard_mismatches ---");
    131                                              
    132                                                      // Test 1: Write transaction to establish baseline
    133             1                          4             t_write = apb_base_seq_item::type_id::create("t_write");
    134             1                          4             t_write.apb_tr = apb_base_seq_item::WRITE;

    138                                              
    139                                                      // Test 2: Read matching transaction (should pass)

    145

    147             1                          4             t_read = apb_base_seq_item::type_id::create("t_uninit1");

    98                                                   // Task to run basic verification sequences
    99                                                   task run_basic_sequences();
    100                                                      apb_master_seq master_seq;  // Base master sequence (mixed R/W)
    101                                                      apb_slave_seq  slave_seq;   // Slave response sequence
    102             1                         20             repeat(5) begin
    103             1                         20                 master_seq = apb_master_seq::type_id::create("master_seq");
    104             1                         20                 slave_seq  = apb_slave_seq::type_id::create("slave_seq");
    105                                                          fork
    106             1                         20                     master_seq.start(env.master_agent.m_sequencer);  // Drive transactions
    107             1                         20                     slave_seq.start(env.slave_agent.m_sequencer);    // Provide responses
    108                                                          join
    109             1                         20                 #10ns;  // Inter-transaction delay
    110                                                      end
    111                                                  endtask;

    51              1                          4             vif.PSEL <= 1'b0; vif.PENABLE <= 1'b0;  // IDLE state
    51              2                          4     
    52              1                          4             @(posedge vif.PCLK);
    53              1                          4             vif.PSEL <= 1'b0; vif.PENABLE <= 1'b1;  // Invalid state (PSEL=0, PENABLE=1)
    53              2                          4     
    54              1                          4             @(posedge vif.PCLK);
    55              1                          4             vif.PENABLE <= 1'b0;                    // Return to IDLE
    56              1                          4             @(posedge vif.PCLK);
    57                                                       
    58                                                       // Test repeated signal patterns
    59              1                         20             repeat(5) begin
    60              1                         20                 @(posedge vif.PCLK);
    61              1                         20                 vif.PSEL <= 1'b0; vif.PENABLE <= 1'b1;  // Invalid state repeated
    61              2                         20     
    62              1                         20                 @(posedge vif.PCLK);
    63              1                         20                 vif.PENABLE <= 1'b0;                    // Return to IDLE
    64              1                         20                 @(posedge vif.PCLK);
    65                                                       end
    66                                                   
    67              1                          4             phase.drop_objection(this);
    68                                                   endtask
    69                                               endclass
